create table teammember(
id varchar(20) primary key,
passwd varchar(20),
name varchar(20),
email varchar(40),
phone varchar(30),
zipcode varchar(20),
address varchar(100),
job varchar(20))charset=utf8;

create table teamboard(
num int(5) primary key, name varchar(20) not null, 
pass varchar(20) not null, mail varchar(30),
title varchar(50), cont text, bip varchar(20), 
bdate varchar(20), readcnt int(3),
gnum int(5), onum int(3), nested int(3)) charset=utf8;

create table player(
no int(5) primary key not null auto_increment,
name varchar(20),price varchar(20),detail text,
sdate datetime,image varchar(20)) charset=utf8;

create table team_product(
no int(5) primary key not null auto_increment,
name varchar(20),price varchar(20),detail text,
sdate datetime,stock varchar(10),image varchar(20)) charset=utf8;

create table team_order(
no int(5) primary key not null auto_increment,
product_no varchar(5) not null,quantity varchar(10),sdate datetime,
state varchar(10),id varchar(20)) charset=utf8;

create table administ(
admin_id varchar(20) primary key not null,
admin_passwd varchar(20) not null) charset=utf8;

zipcode char(7),
area1 varchar(10),
area2 varchar(20),
area3 varchar(30),
area4 varchar(50))charset=utf8;
